Introduction to OC16 Year 1 Semester 1 
 
OC16 is a two-year licensing program  which is  the culmination of Ra's 
investigation into trans-auric forms.   
 
Year One: WA Theoretics 
In year one, this program focuses on the correlation between WA mechanics 
and basic human organizing patterns.  WA mechanics determine both tribal 
and gene pool formation and provide frameworks for the establishment of 
successful groupings. 
 
Semester 1  introduces you to the trans -auric WA, the alpha, and the 
organizing channels of the superior and inferior pentas as well as their 
power bases.  
 
Pre-requisite:  
The year one program is open to certified BG5 Consultants, IHDS Certified 
professional Analysts and Teachers and to third year Science of 
Differentiation College students.  
 
 
 
Year Two: OC16 Corporate & Large Group Analysis 
Year Two is only open to BG5 Consultants who have completed year one.

Theoretics One  
The Trans-Auric WA 
 
I must say that it's something I've been looking forward to for a very long time.  
Actually there are only two people who ever had any detailed information from me 
about the nature of OC16, about the nature of the 
WA, the way in which it operates in the wo rld, 
and the way in which it impacts literally 
everything.  It's something that has waited its 
time.  I've had the privilege of being able to go 
through in detail all of the various form s and did 
give a short course on the WA  two or three years 
ago, if I remember. 
 
This is something that really is the crown at the 
top of this whole process of unraveling the form 
principle on the planet, because what we're really 
talking about here is the coordinating agency of 
the form principle on the planet.  And that's t he 
coordinating agency for the form principle as it operates through us.  It is something 
that, I guess in a way, because of course  the moment I suggest any of these things 
it can be taken as an absolute.  This is what makes our existence possible.  It has to 
be coordinated.   
 
It's the most fascinat ing thing about movement.  The fact that we are all objects 
moving in space, the coordination of this is a Monopole game.  And the Monopole 
game is played out in many ways.  It's played out through individual an d individual 
attractive value to the other.  It's the glue that holds families together, groups 
together, tribes together and so forth and so on. 
 
The WA is the Bedrock of the Success of Our Species  
What we're looking at here is something that was absolut ely fundamental to the 
beginning of the success of our species.  And the success of our species was not 
something that was determined until we were able to establish a viable WA.  That is, 
a viable in our language or what will be our language, OC16, becaus e this is the very 
bedrock.  It is , in and of itself , not sufficient.  What we will see is that the moment 
you bring five of these trans-auric WAs together is the moment you lay the 
foundation for the gene pool itself.  In other words, it is the moment tha t you lay 
down the viability of any particular grouping. 
 
Everything about life on this planet, if we go back in our evolutionary history, if we 
go back to—and pardon creationists, they drive me crazy , this nonsense; anyway, 
sorry, it just popped in there—if you go all the way back, what you're looking at is an

organizing principle that was all organized around the trans-auric.  Everything about 
the trans-auric is that it is so different from the personal auric, like you and me with 
our personal self -contained auras, and the assumption that we are unitary, at least 
in the way we perceive this.   
 
We are closed auras, like the mammals, like the insects, like the plants, like the 
cells.  C losed in an illusion, if we want, of singularity.   It's so different from the 
trans-auric form.  It's so different from the foundation of the trans-auric form which 
is the Penta.  This is the absolute foundation of everything.  
 
The Penta is an Electromagnetic Entity  
The fact is that the WA is something t hat has an ability to emerge out of the 
convergence of Pentas.  But the Penta is the priority because the Penta is the trans-
auric foundation.  And it is not like you and me.  It isn't, even when you belong to 
one, because it isn't like us.  It does not li ve in this kind of vehicular construct.  It is 
an electromagnetic entity.  It has no centers and  it has no gates, not in the sense 
that we understand it.  It is form that is in movement that morphs constantly. 
 
But we have an advantage.  I love the advantage.  The advantage is that I was given 
the design of forms.  I was given a mechanical layout, the blueprints, if you will.  In 
being able to have the blueprint, one can begin to grasp certain things.  At this point 
in my career , I have taught  BG5 for three  years.  I've taught many, many family 
Penta programs and cour ses over the years.  I have  a deep familiarity with the 
nature of the Penta itself.   
 
And yet, the Penta itself, for so many people, particularly those who are new to any 
kind of Penta understa nding, it takes awhile to begin to understand how alien the 
trans-auric form is.  And that in its very alien -ness it gives us what is fundamentally 
a direction that is more powerful than what lies within the individual.  It's powerful 
glue, this stuff.  We  know it best with family.  We know it best when somebody says 
that you can love a parent, a sibling, a child without liking them, this kind of stuff.  
The glue that is there in a Penta holds you together in a relative harmony.  It does 
depend on whether there is a gap in the 46 or not, but literally holds you together in 
this relative harmony and it's a very powerful glue.   
 
It is essential to see that we as individuals have never been given empowerment.  
It's never been in the program.  No matter what the illusion is.  It certainly never 
existed for the seven -centered being, never existed at all.  It's only now.  It's only 
since the advent of this.  It's only with the possibility of nine -centered consciousness 
that we reach a place where it's possible f or us to live out what is a unique formula 
within the context of the way in which the maia operates.  
 
And yet, the ma ia is totally determined by the trans-auric.  Appropriate, is it not?  
What is not seen, what no one has any natural , conscious awareness of, that these 
invisible mechanisms are controlling everything.  It sou nds like science fiction.  But 
the longer you understand Penta and the deeper you watch Penta , the more the

shivers go up and down your spine because you get to see, oh my goodness.  Oh , I

The Trans-Auric is Uni-directional 
When you look at a Penta you know it has no awareness, and it has no ego either.  
It's so different.  The trans-auric form is so different from us because it is uni-
directional.  We're not.  We're not at all, as a ma tter of fact.  Everything about us, 
everything about the nature of the way in which we are designed is in that nature 
energy within our 
individual design can 
go in any direction.  
It can go up, it can 
go down, and it  can 
go sideways.   It can 
do all those t hings. 
The flow within the 
64-gate matrix is 
multi-directional. 
 
But the moment you 
get into the Penta , 
it's all unidirectional, 
all one direction all 
going up, all one 
direction.  It's totally 
different from us.  
It's totally different 
from every other 
living thing because 
every other living 
thing that is within 
an enclosed aura, all of them are multi -directional in the way energy and information 
flows within their system.  But that's not true with the trans-auric form.  Energy only 
moves in one direction.  
 
Think about what that means just at the common sense level .  When you enter into 
a Penta, you lose a major option in your existence, an option that governs the most 
important thing that a human being has.  Human Design presents Strategy and 
Authority for one reason:  to be able to refine and perfect the way in which one 
makes decisions which is navigation in space.  This navigation, this direction , is 
something you have a right to create out of what is correct for you in terms of your 
Strategy and Authority.

But the moment that you step into a Penta, a Penta is dominated by direction; it's 
pulling.  And it pulls everything in and it strips away that other option.  It strips away 
the individual direction.  How many sacrifices have you made for your fam ily?  How 
many roads have you taken because they're not your road?  Because you are bound 
to the glue of the Penta , it takes great strength and discipline and correctness within  
yourself to resist such things.  But they are there , and if you are not aware,  if you 
are not vigilant, you watch and see how it pulls you along until you get to that place 
where you say, ―Why am I here?   How the hell did I get  here?  I don’t want to be 
here." 
 
Penta is a living thing and it doesn't give a hoot about you.  It's clea r to me that in 
no sense is it aware of you.  The trans-auric form takes a view, bits and pieces.  It's 
sort of like a Frankenstein —I don't mean to paint a dark, ugly or anything picture, 
but it gives you an idea.  It's these bits and pieces that  it pulls electromagnetically 
from your aura.  It doesn't take all of you.  It's why you always feel when you're 
growing up that nobody knows you; nobody sees you because you're always 
somehow controlled in the way you react and behave within the conditioning of 
whatever the Penta happens to be. 
 
The Penta Harmonizes the Auras  
Those of you who are familiar with Penta know that the dilemmas in Penta, the 
openness in Penta, the gaps in Penta lead to energy being placed into those areas 
and becomes the domina nt theme in any kind of grouping.  Your individuality, your 
uniqueness does not exist.  Think about this, not now, but go back deep, deep, deep, 
deep into history.  Go back when the force to bond was of deep value as a survival 
mechanism.  These early group ings, these early Pentas had a uniform and defined 
direction that you did not want to be out of it.  As we know, one of the things the 
Penta does that is really, for me, so incredible is that the major work of the Penta, in 
order for it to be truly successful, is the ability to harmonize the auras. 
 
You had those five in the cave that had a harmony amongst them that was not a 
natural harmony.  It was not natural in the sense there was not any predisposed bon  
ami for each other.  It's what Penta does.  It's like a drug.  The Penta , in a sense, is 
sedating you.  And in your sedation , it takes from you precisely what it needs to do 
its work, not yours. 
 
One of the reasons I have been looking forward to this adventure is that I've tried to 
show the nature, the depth and the insidiousness of the control of the Program in 
everything I teach.  For me , it is the essential truth revealed in this knowledge, that 
there is this vast, vast infrastructure that literally organizes the vast majority of what 
is taking place on this plane.  It says clearly in all of that, that there is only one thing 
you can d o, save yourself, because the conditioning is incredible and here you're 
going to enter into the land of ultimate conditioning.  It is a place that nobody else

The Nature of the Word Inferior 
Hello to all of you and welcome.  And welcome to the Inferior Penta.  I was making a 
comment before the class started about the nature of this word.  One of the things I 
was commenting on is the language in Human Design, a language that is built on 
and bui lt out of the mechanics.  So we have a very specific way in which we use 
words.  Inferior has certain connotations, obviously, and it's one that can be brought 
to this particular configuration.   
 
I think it's very important to understand something about the Inferior Penta.  It is 
Inferior relative to the Superior Penta, and nothing else.  And that is something that 
we'll discuss later as we move along, because it will help us understand how 
successful OC16, how a WA can actually be established that is  really viable and 
operates correctly.

Program, which is what I’m really exploring now, to see the way the Program is 
manipulated.  All of this is just a mechanism.  It’s why we’re here in WA Theoretics.  
It’s not about what we’re going to be able to do at the m undane level when we 
ignore what the WA represents, what we ignore in terms of what it represents to the 
possibility of a unique individual.  But OC16 as a large group analysis system is just 
simply about making those WAs work better, function better, and be more successful 
within the homogenized frame. 
 
I have nothing against that.  I have nothing against efficiency.  I have nothing 
against human beings who are never going to get it, getting at least some sense 
within the homogenized world that they think that life is pretty ok for them.  After 
all, this knowledge is here to serve at many, many levels.  For most human beings it 
will never be their fractal.  It will never, ever, ever be their fractal to come even 
close to what is possible for a unique being.  They just won’t.   
 
But it doesn’t mean that there isn’t something that can be done for them.  We see 
that in Penta.  You create a functional Penta, everybody enjoys their work, and 
everybody has a little more success.  On that level it makes human being s happy.  It 
gives them a sense of well-being in their lives.  But it’s all relative.  They still have all 
that darkness within them.  They still have all the dilemmas that are there in the 
not-self consciousness. 
 
The Program Comes Alive in the WA

The Program is not just a concept; it’s alive in the WA.  It’s where the Program

It means that we begin to have a totally differ ent understanding of incarnation when

see the WA, this is the basic overview of how life is organized.  So, at this lev el 
you're really beginning to be able to integrate all the knowledge that you have.  It's 
a great format for understanding the way in which humanity operates. 
 
And obviously with the direction you're taking in terms of the OC16 from the 
application point of view, the more you experience this, the more you ponder it, the 
more you watch your own relationship to it, this is something that is important.  But 
again, my caution, you really have to do that with awareness. 
 
Working from Home and the WA 
Question:  So you know in the United States and probably other countries too, I'm 
just more familiar with the US there's been such a rise of working from home, even if 
you work for a corporation.  Do you see that as a part of the breaking down of the 
infrastructure with the 19/49 as we're moving towards the 2027 and people really 
trying to pull away from WAs? 
 
Ra:  My intuitive feeling about that, Cathy, because it is a good point, is that there is 
my constant referral to the 4% of the 4%.  You have to be outside of th e WA to even 
begin to have a chance.  You have to be basically outside of the Penta to be able to 
have a chance to confront yourself to a point that perhaps the door can open for you.  
And I think that one of the things that we're seeing in the way in whic h the Program 
is working because it is a short window, that is, the phenomena that we see today, 
this working at home, is in many ways a precursor of there isn't going to be any 
organized environment. 
 
But I think it serves another purpose.  That is, I thi nk it provides opportunities, as I 
mentioned about the virtual, I think it really provides opportunities for those that 
don't really fit in.  After all, only certain people can really work at home.  Not 
everybody can do that.  You have to be very disciplin ed.  You have to be very 
respectful about the nature of your work.  There are a lot of things that go with it.  
There's nobody, obviously, looking over your shoulder, there are all these kinds of 
things.  So, these beings already have a very individual con trol over their process.  
They're really fertile ground for transformation. 
 
Alone in a Flat in a Multistory House 
Question:  If I am alone in a flat, but the flat still in a multistory house, I'm not 
clear, am I still in a WA, despite the fact that I am not in a Penta in the flat? 
 Theoretics Eleven 
The WA  
The OC 16 is a program of the International Human Design School (IHDS) 
All Rights Reserved.  Copyright 2008 Jovian Archive Corporation 
177 
 
Ra:  If you're in a flat and there are other people in the building, all of those auras 
ultimately connect to each other in one way or another.  There is always the WA 
influence on anyone who is living in those environments.   It's not like you're always 
in the WA.  As a matter of fact, it will come and it will go.  It will depend on how 
many people are around you and above you.  It may only be Penta that is 
happening.  But you're living in what is fundamentally a WA environment a nd you're 
always going to be influenced by it.  It doesn't matter whether you're alone in your 
flat. 
 
All right, as always I want to thank you.  It's been a very enjoyable semester.  I look 
forward to our continuing journey which is you will see is quite something as well.  
And by the way, thank you Adrian for those stats; they're fascinating as always.  T o 
all of you, you take care.  Have yourself a good break and enjoy it.  Beware of WAs, 
wherever they are.  Thanks again.  Until next time, you take care, bye for now.  
 
 
 
 
~The End of OC 16 Year 1 Semester 1~
